guestbook/guestbook.py \u304c\u3042\u308a\uff0c\u30da\u30fc\u30b8\u306e\u30d5\u30c3\u30bf\u30fc\u306b\u30c7\u30fc\u30bf\u30b9\u30c8\u30a2\u306e\u6328\u62f6\u3092\u683c\u7d0d\u3057\u3066\u3044\u307e\u3059\u3002\u6b8b\u308a\u306e\u30da\u30fc\u30b8\u3067\u306f\u65b0\u3057\u3044\u3053\u3068\u3092\u8b70\u8ad6\u3057\u307e\u3059\u3002\n\nguestbook.py\nimport cgi\nimport urllib\n\nfrom google.appengine.api import users\nfrom google.appengine.ext import ndb\n\nimport webapp2\n\n\nMAIN_PAGE_FOOTER_TEMPLATE = \"\"\"\\\n    <form action=\"/sign?%s\" method=\"post\">\n      <div><textarea name=\"content\" rows=\"3\" cols=\"60\"></textarea></div>\n      <div><input type=\"submit\" value=\"Sign Guestbook\"></div>\n    </form>\n\n    <hr>\n\n    <form>Guestbook name:\n      <input value=\"%s\" name=\"guestbook_name\">\n      <input type=\"submit\" value=\"switch\">\n    </form>\n\n    <a href=\"%s\">%s</a>\n\n  </body>\n</html>\n\"\"\"\n\nDEFAULT_GUESTBOOK_NAME = 'default_guestbook'\n\n\n# We set a parent key on the 'Greetings' to ensure that they are all in the same\n# entity group. Queries across the single entity group will be consistent.\n# However, the write rate should be limited to ~1/second.\n\ndef guestbook_key(guestbook_name=DEFAULT_GUESTBOOK_NAME):\n    \"\"\"Constructs a Datastore key for a Guestbook entity with guestbook_name.\"\"\"\n    return ndb.Key('Guestbook', guestbook_name)\n\n\nclass Greeting(ndb.Model):\n    \"\"\"Models an individual Guestbook entry with author, content, and date.\"\"\"\n    author = ndb.UserProperty()\n    content = ndb.StringProperty(indexed=False)\n    date = ndb.DateTimeProperty(auto_now_add=True)\n\n\nclass MainPage(webapp2.RequestHandler):\n\n    def get(self):\n        self.response.write('<html><body>')\n        guestbook_name = self.request.get('guestbook_name',\n                                          DEFAULT_GUESTBOOK_NAME)\n\n        # Ancestor Queries, as shown here, are strongly consistent with the High\n        # Replication Datastore. Queries that span entity groups are eventually\n        # consistent. If we omitted the ancestor from this query there would be\n        # a slight chance that Greeting that had just been written would not\n        # show up in a query.\n        greetings_query = Greeting.query(\n            ancestor=guestbook_key(guestbook_name)).order(-Greeting.date)\n        greetings = greetings_query.fetch(10)\n\n        for greeting in greetings:\n            if greeting.author:\n                self.response.write(\n                        '<b>%s</b> wrote:' % greeting.author.nickname())\n            else:\n                self.response.write('An anonymous person wrote:')\n            self.response.write('<blockquote>%s</blockquote>' %\n                                cgi.escape(greeting.content))\n\n        if users.get_current_user():\n            url = users.create_logout_url(self.request.uri)\n            url_linktext = 'Logout'\n        else:\n            url = users.create_login_url(self.request.uri)\n            url_linktext = 'Login'\n\n        # Write the submission form and the footer of the page\n        sign_query_params = urllib.urlencode({'guestbook_name': guestbook_name})\n        self.response.write(MAIN_PAGE_FOOTER_TEMPLATE %\n                            (sign_query_params, cgi.escape(guestbook_name),\n                             url, url_linktext))\n\n\nclass Guestbook(webapp2.RequestHandler):\n\n    def post(self):\n        # We set the same parent key on the 'Greeting' to ensure each Greeting\n        # is in the same entity group. Queries across the single entity group\n        # will be consistent. However, the write rate to a single entity group\n        # should be limited to ~1/second.\n        guestbook_name = self.request.get('guestbook_name',\n                                          DEFAULT_GUESTBOOK_NAME)\n        greeting = Greeting(parent=guestbook_key(guestbook_name))\n\n        if users.get_current_user():\n            greeting.author = users.get_current_user()\n\n        greeting.content = self.request.get('content')\n        greeting.put()\n\n        query_params = {'guestbook_name': guestbook_name}\n        self.redirect('/?' + urllib.urlencode(query_params))\n\n\napplication = webapp2.WSGIApplication([\n    ('/', MainPage),\n    ('/sign', Guestbook),\n], debug=True)\n\n\nguestbook/guestbook.py Queries across the single entity group\n        # will be consistent. greeting.content = self.request.get('content')\n        greeting.put()\n\n        query_params = {'guestbook_name': guestbook_name}\n        self.redirect('/?' +         url = users.create_logout_url(self.request.uri)\n            url_linktext = 'Logout'\n        else:\n            url = users.create_login_url(self.request.uri)\n            url_linktext = self.response.write(template.render(template_values))\n\n\n\u6700\u5f8c\u306b\uff0c\u65b0\u3057\u3044\u30d5\u30a1\u30a4\u30eb\u3092 guestbook \u3092\u3082\u3046\u4e00\u5ea6\u7de8\u96c6\u3057\u3066\uff0c\u4e2d\u8eab\u3092\u6b21\u306e\u3088\u3046\u306b\u7f6e\u304d\u63db\u3048\u3066\u307f\u3066\u304f\u3060\u3055\u3044\u3002\n\n```py:helloworld.py\nfrom self.response.headers['Content-Type'] = 'text/plain'\n            self.response.write('Hello, ' + user.nickname())\n        else:\n            self.redirect(users.create_login_url(self.request.uri))\n\n\napplication = webapp2.WSGIApplication([\n    ('/', MainPage),\n], debug=True)\n```\n\n\u30d6\u30e9\u30a6\u30b6\u306e\u30da\u30fc\u30b8\u3092\u66f4\u65b0\u3057\u3066\u304f\u3060\u3055\u3044\u3002\u30a2\u30d7\u30ea\u30b1\u30fc\u30b7\u30e7\u30f3\u306f\u30c6\u30b9\u30c8\u3059\u308b\u306e\u306b\u9069\u3057\u305f\u30ed\u30fc\u30ab\u30eb\u7248\u306e Google \u306e\u30b5\u30a4\u30f3\u30a4\u30f3\u306e\u30da\u30fc\u30b8\u306b\u30ea\u30c0\u30a4\u30ec\u30af\u30c8\u3057\u3066\u304f\u308c\u307e\u3059\u3002\u541b\u306f\u597d\u304d\u306a\u30e6\u30fc\u30b6\u540d\u3092\u3053\u306e\u753b\u9762\u3067\u5165\u529b\u3067\u304d\uff0c\u30a2\u30d7\u30ea\u30b1\u30fc\u30b7\u30e7\u30f3\u306f\u4eee\u306e\u30e6\u30fc\u30b6\u3092\u30e6\u30fc\u30b6\u540d\u306b\u57fa\u3044\u3066\u8868\u793a\u3057\u3066\u304f\u308c\u307e\u3059\u3002\n\n\u30a2\u30d7\u30ea\u30b1\u30fc\u30b7\u30e7\u30f3\u304c App Engine \u3067\u52d5\u304f\u3068\u304d\u306f\uff0c\u30e6\u30fc\u30b6\u306f Google \u30a2\u30ab\u30a6\u30f3\u30c8\u306e\u30b5\u30a4\u30f3\u30a4\u30f3\u306e\u30da\u30fc\u30b8\u306b\u30ea\u30c0\u30a4\u30ec\u30af\u30c8\u3055\u308c\u3066\uff0c\u30b5\u30a4\u30f3\u30a4\u30f3\u306b\u6210\u529f\u3059\u308b\u304b\u30a2\u30ab\u30a6\u30f3\u30c8\u3092\u4f5c\u6210\u3057\u305f\u3042\u3068\u306b\u30a2\u30d7\u30ea\u30b1\u30fc\u30b7\u30e7\u30f3\u306b\u30b3\u30fc\u30eb\u30d0\u30c3\u30af\u3057\u307e\u3059\u3002\n\n##Users API\n\n\n\u305d\u3046\u3057\u305f\u3089\u65b0\u3057\u3044\u90e8\u5206\u3092\u898b\u3066\u3044\u304d\u307e\u3057\u3087\u3046\u3002\n\n```py\nuser = users.get_current_user()\n```\n\n\u3082\u3057\u30e6\u30fc\u30b6\u304c\u65e2\u306b\u30b5\u30a4\u30f3\u30a4\u30f3\u6e08\u307f\u306a\u3089\uff0cget_current_user() \u306f User \u30aa\u30d6\u30b8\u30a7\u30af\u30c8\u3092\u30e6\u30fc\u30b6\u306b\u8fd4\u3057\u307e\u3059\u3002\u305d\u3046\u3067\u306a\u3051\u308c\u3070 None \u3092\u8fd4\u3057\u307e\u3059\u3002\n\n```py\nif user:\n    self.response.headers['Content-Type'] = 'text/plain'\n    self.response.write('Hello, ' + user.nickname())\n```\n\n\u3082\u3057\u30e6\u30fc\u30b6\u304c\u30b5\u30a4\u30f3\u30a4\u30f3\u6e08\u307f\u306a\u3089\uff0c\u30e6\u30fc\u30b6\u30a2\u30ab\u30a6\u30f3\u30c8\u306b\u7d10\u4ed8\u3051\u3089\u308c\u305f\u30cb\u30c3\u30af\u30cd\u30fc\u30e0\u3092\u4f7f\u7528\u3057\u3066\u500b\u5225\u306e\u30e1\u30c3\u30bb\u30fc\u30b8\u3092\u8868\u793a\u3057\u307e\u3059\u3002\n\n```py\nelse:\n   self.redirect(users.create_login_url(self.request.uri))\n```\n\n\u3082\u3057\u30e6\u30fc\u30b6\u304c\u30b5\u30a4\u30f3\u30a4\u30f3\u3057\u3066\u3044\u306a\u3051\u308c\u3070\uff0cwebapp2 \u306b\u30e6\u30fc\u30b6\u306e\u30d6\u30e9\u30a6\u30b6\u3092 Google \u30a2\u30ab\u30a6\u30f3\u30c8\u306e\u30b5\u30a4\u30f3\u30a4\u30f3\u753b\u9762\u306b\u30ea\u30c0\u30a4\u30ec\u30af\u30c8\u3059\u308b\u3088\u3046\u306b\u4f1d\u3048\u307e\u3059\u3002\u30ea\u30c0\u30a4\u30ec\u30af\u30c8\u306b\u306f\u305d\u308c\u81ea\u8eab\u306e\u30da\u30fc\u30b8 ( self.request.uri ) \u3078\u306e URL \u304c\u542b\u307e\u308c\uff0cGoogle \u30c7\u30a3\u30ec\u30af\u30c8\u30ea\u3092\u4f7f\u3063\u3066\u3044\u3053\u3046\u3002\n\n##webapp2 \u3067 Web \u30d5\u30a9\u30fc\u30e0\u3092\u6271\u3046\n\napp.yaml \u306e libraries webapp2\n  version: latest\n```\n\nguestbook/guestbook.py \u306e\u5185\u5bb9\u3092\u6b21\u306e\u3088\u3046\u306b\u7f6e\u304d\u63db\u3048\u3066\u304f\u3060\u3055\u3044\u3002\n\n```py:guestbook.py\nimport cgi\n\nfrom google.appengine.api import users\n\nimport webapp2\n\n\nMAIN_PAGE_HTML = \"\"\"\\\n<html>\n  <body>\n    <form action=\"/sign\" method=\"post\">\n      <div><textarea name=\"content\" rows=\"3\" cols=\"60\"></textarea></div>\n      <div><input type=\"submit\" value=\"Sign Guestbook\"></div>\n    </form>\n  </body>\n</html>\n\"\"\"\n\n\nclass MainPage(webapp2.RequestHandler):\n\n    def get(self):\n        self.response.write(MAIN_PAGE_HTML)\n\n\nclass Guestbook(webapp2.RequestHandler):\n\n    def post(self):\n        self.response.write('<html><body>You wrote:<pre>')\n        self.response.write(cgi.escape(self.request.get('content')))\n        self.response.write('</pre></body></html>')\n\n\napplication = webapp2.WSGIApplication([\n    ('/', MainPage),\n    ('/sign', \u306e\u88cf\u3067\u30c7\u30fc\u30bf\u3092\u8ca0\u8377\u5206\u6563\u3057\u307e\u3059\u3002\u5f37\u529b\u306a\u30af\u30a8\u30ea\u30a8\u30f3\u30b8\u30f3\u3068\u30c8\u30e9\u30f3\u30b6\u30af\u30b7\u30e7\u30f3\u3092\u624b\u306b\u3057\u307e\u3057\u3087\u3046\u3002\n\nApp u306b\u9650\u3089\u308c\u305f\u3082\u306e\u306f\u5e38\u306b\u6700\u65b0\u306e[\u5f37\u3044\u6574\u5408\u6027](http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Strong_consistency)\u3092\u6301\u3064\u7d50\u679c\u3092\u8fd4\u3059\u3002\n\n\u3053\u306e\u30ac\u30a4\u30c9\u306e\u30b3\u30fc\u30c9\u30b5\u30f3\u30d7\u30eb\u306f\u30a8\u30f3\u30c6\u30a3\u30c6\u30a3\u30b0\u30eb\u30fc\u30d7\u306b\u95a2\u9023\u3059\u308b\u30a8\u30f3\u30c6\u30a3\u30c6\u30a3\u3092\u6574\u7406\u3057\u3066\uff0c\u305d\u308c\u3089\u306e\u30a8\u30f3\u30c6\u30a3\u30c6\u30a3\u30b0\u30eb\u30fc\u30d7\u306e\u5148\u7956\u554f\u3044\u5408\u308f\u305b\u3092\u5f37\u3044\u6574\u5408\u6027\u306e\u3042\u308b\u7d50\u679c\u3092\u8fd4\u3059\u305f\u3081\u306b\u4f7f\u3044\u307e\u3059\u3002\u30b5\u30f3\u30d7\u30eb\u30b3\u30fc\u30c9\u306e\u30b3\u30e1\u30f3\u30c8\u3067\u306f\uff0c\u3044\u304f\u3064\u304b\u30a2\u30d7\u30ea\u30b1\u30fc\u30b7\u30e7\u30f3\u306e\u8a2d\u8a08\u306b\u5f71\u97ff\u3092\u4e0e\u3048\u308b\u53ef\u80fd\u6027\u306e\u3042\u308b\uff0c\u3044\u304f\u3064\u304b\u306e\u65b9\u6cd5\u3092\u5f37\u8abf\u3057\u3066\u3044\u307e\u3059(\u8a33\u8005\u6ce8\uff1a\"this\"\u306f\"that\"\u306e\u8aa4\u690d\u3068\u5224\u65ad)\u3002\u8a73\u7d30\u306f\uff0c[\u5f37\u3044\u6574\u5408\u6027\u306e\u3042\u308b\u30c7\u30fc\u30bf\u69cb\u7bc9](https://developers.google.com/appengine/docs/python/datastore/structuring_for_strong_consistency?hl=ja)\u3092\u898b\u3066\u304f\u3060\u3055\u3044\u3002\n\n##\u30c7\u30fc\u30bf\u30b9\u30c8\u30a2\u3092\u5229\u7528\u3057\u305f\u5b8c\u5168\u306a\u4f8b\n\n\u3053\u3053\u306b\u65b0\u3057\u3044\u30d0\u30fc\u30b8\u30e7\u30f3\u306e guestbook/guestbook.py \u304c\u3042\u308a\uff0c\u30da\u30fc\u30b8\u306e\u30d5\u30c3\u30bf\u30fc\u306b\u30c7\u30fc\u30bf\u30b9\u30c8\u30a2\u306e\u6328\u62f6\u3092\u683c\u7d0d\u3057\u3066\u3044\u307e\u3059\u3002\u6b8b\u308a\u306e\u30da\u30fc\u30b8\u3067\u306f\u65b0\u3057\u3044\u3053\u3068\u3092\u8b70\u8ad6\u3057\u307e\u3059\u3002\n\n```py:guestbook.py\nimport cgi\nimport urllib\n\nfrom google.appengine.api import users\nfrom google.appengine.ext import ndb\n\nimport webapp2\n\n\nMAIN_PAGE_FOOTER_TEMPLATE = \"\"\"\\\n    <form action=\"/sign?%s\" method=\"post\">\n      <div><textarea name=\"content\" rows=\"3\" cols=\"60\"></textarea></div>\n      <div><input type=\"submit\" value=\"Sign Guestbook\"></div>\n    </form>\n\n    <hr>\n\n    <form>Guestbook name:\n      <input value=\"%s\" name=\"guestbook_name\">\n      <input type=\"submit\" value=\"switch\">\n    </form>\n\n    <a href=\"%s\">%s</a>\n\n  </body>\n</html>\n\"\"\"\n\nDEFAULT_GUESTBOOK_NAME = 'default_guestbook'\n\n\n# We set a parent key on the 'Greetings' to ensure that they are all in the same\n# entity group. Queries across the single entity group will be consistent.\n# However, the write rate should be limited to ~1/second.\n\ndef guestbook_key(guestbook_name=DEFAULT_GUESTBOOK_NAME):\n    \"\"\"Constructs a Datastore key for a Guestbook entity with guestbook_name.\"\"\"\n    return ndb.Key('Guestbook', guestbook_name)\n\n\nclass Greeting(ndb.Model):\n    \"\"\"Models an individual Guestbook entry with author, content, and date.\"\"\"\n    author = ndb.UserProperty()\n    content = ndb.StringProperty(indexed=False)\n    date = ndb.DateTimeProperty(auto_now_add=True)\n\n\nclass MainPage(webapp2.RequestHandler):\n\n    def get(self):\n        self.response.write('<html><body>')\n        guestbook_name = self.request.get('guestbook_name',\n                                          DEFAULT_GUESTBOOK_NAME)\n\n        # Ancestor Queries, as shown here, are strongly consistent with the High\n        # Replication Datastore. Queries that span entity groups are eventually\n        # consistent. If we omitted the ancestor from this query there would be\n        # a slight chance that Greeting that had just been written would not\n        # show up in a query.\n        greetings_query = Greeting.query(\n            ancestor=guestbook_key(guestbook_name)).order(-Greeting.date)\n        greetings = greetings_query.fetch(10)\n\n        for greeting in greetings:\n            if greeting.author:\n                self.response.write(\n                        '<b>%s</b> wrote:' % greeting.author.nickname())\n            else:\n                self.response.write('An anonymous person wrote:')\n            self.response.write('<blockquote>%s</blockquote>' %\n                                cgi.escape(greeting.content))\n\n        if users.get_current_user():\n            url = users.create_logout_url(self.request.uri)\n            url_linktext = 'Logout'\n        else:\n            url = users.create_login_url(self.request.uri)\n            url_linktext = 'Login'\n\n        # Write the submission form and the footer of the page\n        sign_query_params = urllib.urlencode({'guestbook_name': guestbook_name})\n        self.response.write(MAIN_PAGE_FOOTER_TEMPLATE %\n                            (sign_query_params, cgi.escape(guestbook_name),\n                             url, url_linktext))\n\n\nclass Guestbook(webapp2.RequestHandler):\n\n    def post(self):\n        # We set the same parent key on the 'Greeting' to ensure each Greeting\n        # is in the same entity group. Queries across the single entity group\n        # will be consistent. However, the write rate to a single entity group\n        # should be limited to ~1/second.\n        guestbook_name = self.request.get('guestbook_name',\n                                          DEFAULT_GUESTBOOK_NAME)\n        greeting = Greeting(parent=guestbook_key(guestbook_name))\n\n        if users.get_current_user():\n            greeting.author = users.get_current_user()\n\n        greeting.content = self.request.get('content')\n        greeting.put()\n\n        query_params = {'guestbook_name': guestbook_name}\n        self.redirect('/?' + urllib.urlencode(query_params))\n\n\napplication = webapp2.WSGIApplication([\n    ('/', MainPage),\n    ('/sign', Guestbook),\n], debug=True)\n```\n\nguestbook/guestbook.py \u3092\u30ea\u30ed\u30fc\u30c9\u3057\u3066\u304f\u3060\u3055\u3044\u3002\u30e1\u30c3\u30bb\u30fc\u30b8\u304c\u6b63\u3057\u304f\u4fdd\u5b58\uff0c\u8868\u793a\u3055\u308c\u308b\u306e\u3092\u78ba\u8a8d\u3059\u308b\u305f\u3081\u306b\u77ed\u3044\u30e1\u30c3\u30bb\u30fc\u30b8\u3092\u6295\u7a3f\u3057\u3066\u304f\u3060\u3055\u3044\u3002\n\n\u8b66\u544a\uff01\u3000\u30ed\u30fc\u30ab\u30eb\u3067\u306e\u30a2\u30d7\u30ea\u30b1\u30fc\u30b7\u30e7\u30f3\u5185\u306e\u554f\u3044\u5408\u308f\u305b\u306e\u5b9f\u884c\u306f \u304c\u6b20\u3051\u3066\u3044\u308b\u304b\u4e0d\u5b8c\u5168\u306a\u5834\u5408\uff0c\u30a2\u30c3\u30d7\u30ed\u30fc\u30c9\u3057\u305f\u30a2\u30d7\u30ea\u30b1\u30fc\u30b7\u30e7\u30f3\u304c\u554f\u3044\u5408\u308f\u305b\u3092\u5b9f\u884c\u3059\u308b\u3068\u304d\uff0c\u5fc5\u8981\u306a\u30a4\u30f3\u30c7\u30c3\u30af\u30b9\u304c\u6307\u5b9a\u3055\u308c\u3066\u3044\u306a\u3044\u305f\u3081\u306b\u30a4\u30f3\u30c7\u30c3\u30af\u30b9\u30a8\u30e9\u30fc\u304c\u51fa\u307e\u3059\u3002\u5236\u4f5c\u4e2d\u306b\u30a4\u30f3\u30c7\u30c3\u30af\u30b9\u30a8\u30e9\u30fc\u3092\u898b\u9003\u3055\u306a\u3044\u3088\u3046\u306b\uff0c\u5e38\u306b\u65b0\u3057\u3044\u554f\u3044\u5408\u308f\u305b\u3092\u6700\u4f4e\uff11\u56de\u30ed\u30fc\u30ab\u30eb\u3067\u30c6\u30b9\u30c8\u3057\u3066\u304b\u3089\u30a2\u30d7\u30ea\u30b1\u30fc\u30b7\u30e7\u30f3\u3092\u30a2\u30c3\u30d7\u30ed\u30fc\u30c9\u3057\u307e\u3057\u3087\u3046\u3002\u8a73\u7d30\u306f \u30c7\u30fc\u30bf\u30b9\u30c8\u30a2\u30a4\u30f3\u30c7\u30c3\u30af\u30b9\u8a2d\u5b9a](https://developers.google.com/appengine/docs/python/config/indexconfig?hl=ja)\u3092\u898b\u3066\u304f\u3060\u3055\u3044\u3002\n\n##\u9001\u4fe1\u3057\u305f\u6328\u62f6\u306e\u4fdd\u5b58\n\nApp Greeting Guestbook \u30cf\u30f3\u30c9\u30e9\u306f\u65b0\u3057\u3044\u6328\u62f6\u3092\u4f5c\u3063\u3066\u30c7\u30fc\u30bf\u30b9\u30c8\u30a2\u306b\u4fdd\u5b58\u3057\u307e\u3059\u3002\n\n```py\nclass Guestbook(webapp2.RequestHandler):\n\n    def post(self):\n        # We set the same parent key on the 'Greeting' to ensure each Greeting\n        # is in the same entity group. Queries across the single entity group\n        # will be consistent. However, the write rate to a single entity group\n        # should be limited to ~1/second.\n        guestbook_name = self.request.get('guestbook_name',\n                                          DEFAULT_GUESTBOOK_NAME)\n        greeting = Greeting(parent=guestbook_key(guestbook_name))\n\n        if users.get_current_user():\n            greeting.author = users.get_current_user()\n\n        greeting.content = self.request.get('content')\n        greeting.put()\n\n        query_params = {'guestbook_name': guestbook_name}\n        self.redirect('/?' + urllib.urlencode(query_params))\n```\n\n\u3053\u306e\u65b0\u3057\u3044 Guestbook \u30cf\u30f3\u30c9\u30e9\u306f\u65b0\u3057\u3044 Greeting google.appengine.ext import ndb\n\nimport jinja2\nimport webapp2\n\n\nJINJA_ENVIRONMENT = jinja2.Environment(\n    loader=jinja2.FileSystemLoader(os.path.dirname(__file__)),\n    extensions=['jinja2.ext.autoescape'],\n    autoescape=True)\n```\n\nMainPage \u30cf\u30f3\u30c9\u30e9\u3092\u6b21\u306e\u3088\u3046\u306a\u30b3\u30fc\u30c9\u306b\u7f6e\u304d\u63db\u3048\u307e\u3059\u3002\n\n```py:guestbook.py\nclass MainPage(webapp2.RequestHandler):\n\n    def get(self):\n        guestbook_name = self.request.get('guestbook_name',\n                                          DEFAULT_GUESTBOOK_NAME)\n        greetings_query = Greeting.query(\n            ancestor=guestbook_key(guestbook_name)).order(-Greeting.date)\n        greetings = greetings_query.fetch(10)\n\n        if users.get_current_user():\n            url = users.create_logout_url(self.request.uri)\n            url_linktext = 'Logout'\n        else:\n            url = users.create_login_url(self.request.uri)\n            url_linktext = 'Login'\n\n        template_values = {\n            'greetings': greetings,\n            'guestbook_name': urllib.quote_plus(guestbook_name),\n            'url': url,\n            'url_linktext': url_linktext,\n        }\n\n        template = JINJA_ENVIRONMENT.get_template('index.html')\n        self.response.write(template.render(template_values))\n```\n\n\u6700\u5f8c\u306b\uff0c\u65b0\u3057\u3044\u30d5\u30a1\u30a4\u30eb\u3092 guestbook
